D aselmad meqqren i ḥemmlen yinelmaden deg tesdawit, d ameɛnas n tsertit seg zik, d asadur n tarwa n Bennai Weɛli, .... d amɣar yelmed taqbaylit s zreb. Lemmer mačči d widak am kečč iyi-d-ifkan tabɣest i tira deg Tatoeba, seld Tarik Tinouche iyi-d-innan «Aru, ma ad taruḍ, war tugdi !», tili ur ţawḍeɣ ara armi ţxiḍiɣ taqbaylit s tuqqna n wallen. Zik, ţxemmimeɣ ayen ţaruɣ s tṛumit, tura swingimeɣ srid s teqbaylit seld ad aruɣ ye-s. Ayɣer? Acku, d tutlayt-iw tayemmaţ. Wagi yakk, s tejmilt-nwen akken ma tellam! Anef tura i tutlayin-nniḍen am tneglizit i sseqdaceɣ akken aɣ-d-ḍefṛen wiyaḍ: tura ha-ten imarikanen ţgallan kan s yinzan n teqbaylit i d-sseɣtiɣ ar tneglizit, talmanit, tarusit, atg. D asbucceɛ n udlis aqbayli. Akka i walaɣ iswi n tira d-yessalayen iseɣ."

#9526144 "Ungif yeqqaṛ-d ayen yessen, uḥdiq yessen ayen d-yeqqaṛ". Akka i d-yenna yiwen umusnaw. Asteqsi: amusnaw-agi d ungif neɣ d uḥdiq? Ma awal-agi i d-yenna d ayen i yessen, hatan d ungif. Ma s wawal-a, yessen wuḥdiq ayen i d-yeqqaṛ, hatan yella wacu i aɣ-yeffer si tmussni-s! Dɣa amek ara t-namen? Twalam amek ungif yif uḥdiq!
